<div class="Section1">

<span style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">BOOK
TEN</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">ENTITLED
JOANIE;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

</div>

<span
style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">  
</span>

<div class="Section2">

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">REVEALED
AT MECCA<span style="mso-tab-count:3">                                 
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
2">                        </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">In the
name of the most Merciful Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">A.L.R.<a href="#_ftn1" id="_ftnref1"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[1]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.1
These are the signs of this wise Book.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.2 Is
it a strange thing to the women of Mecca, that heaven reveals its
will</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to a
woman that is among you all, saying, “Bring tidings of good news,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even to
those women who will not believe;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and bear
good tidings to those that will believe,”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and on
the merits of their sincerity they have an interest in their Lady of
Light?</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
unbelievers will say, “This is manifest sorcery.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                           
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.3 But
certainly your Lady is Goddess, who has created the heavens and the
earth in six long
days;<a href="#_ftn2" id="_ftnref2"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[2]</span></span></span></span></a>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and then
ascended Her throne, to take on the government of all things. </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">There
is no
intercessor<a href="#_ftn3" id="_ftnref3"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[3]</span></span></span></span></a>,
but only by Her permission.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>You
should carefully consider this.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                 </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.4 To
Her, you shall all return, according to the promise of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for She
produces a creature, and then causes it to return again, to either
heaven or earth,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
She may reward those who believe and those that do right, with
equity.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But as
for the unbelievers, they shall continue to wander the earth without
protection,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">hot
and thirsty for Her love and without a protectress, for they have
disbelieved.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                           
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.5 It
is She who has ordained the sun to shine by day,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
moon shines as a light by night, and She has appointed Her
stations<a href="#_ftn4" id="_ftnref4"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[4]</span></span></span></span></a>,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that you
might know the number of years and the computation of time.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
has created this only with the truth for you.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For
She explains Her signs and miracles to people who understand.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                 
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.6
Moreover. in the changing of night and day,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
whatever Goddess has created in heaven and on earth,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there
are certainly many signs to women who love Her greatly.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.7
Certainly many unbelievers do not care if they meet us at the last
day,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
delight only in the present life, and they rely securely in the same,
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
those who are negligent of signs and miracles from heaven are lost.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.8 For
their dwelling is disorder, and their life is confusion, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they wander, for they have no protectress.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                 
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.9 But
as to those who believe, and work righteousness,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the Lady
of Light will direct them because of their faith;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall have rivers flowing through gardens of pleasure.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.10
Their prayer shall be, “Praise be to You, O Goddess!”</span>

class=Section3&gt;

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And their
greeting to you shall be “Peace!”</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
at the end of their prayers shall be, “Praise be to Goddess, the Lady of
all creatures.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.11 If
other people should cause evil to hasten to women;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">according
to their desire to quickly enrich themselves, certainly they will not be
rewarded.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
we suffer those who hope not to meet at the resurrection, to wander in a
maze of error.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                         
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.12
When evil befalls anyone, she prays lying on her side,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
sitting or standing; but when heaven delivers her from her
affliction,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">she
continues upon her former course of life, as though she had not called
upon Goddess to help her out. This was what the transgressors do.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                                   
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.13
Natural disasters have come and have destroyed many generations who were
before you, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">O women
of Mecca, when they acted wickedly with violence and hatred toward one
another,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">despite
the fact that prophetesses had come to them before with evident
miracles, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and she
had warned them of the disaster which was to come and told them what to
do,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
because she preached only love and tolerance no one would believe</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
hence many were destroyed out of their own stubbornness and hardness of
their hearts.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.14 We
have caused many people to succeed in life,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so when
natural disasters came, their prophetess warned them and instructed them
as to what to do,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet the
unbelievers did not listen and obey, and so they suffered, and many lost
their lives,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this
is so that heaven might see how you would act with wealth and
authority.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Did you use it
wisely?<span style="mso-tab-count:1">           </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.15
When our evident signs and miracles are told to some people,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">those who
hope not to meet the angels at the resurrection say,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Bring a
different Korana from this so we may justify our actions of hate,
violence and war; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or make
some changes so we may oppress others without guilt.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">You
should answer, “It is not fitting for me that I should change this good
Book at my pleasure; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for I
follow only what has been revealed to me, and only peace and love have
been revealed to me.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
I fear, that if I am disobedient to my Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
I should be forgotten and alone on the day of my resurrection.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.16 Say
to the people, “If Goddess had not cared about you, you would not have
received the Korana,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and I
your prophetess would not have taught it to you.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">I
have already dwelt among you all to the age of 45 before I received it.
Do you not understand this?”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">        
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.17 And
who is more unjust than one who devises lies, inspires
oppression,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
teaches war, hate and violence, for all are against the teachings of
Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
they accuse Her signs and miracles of being false. Certainly the wicked
do not prosper in the end.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">             
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.18 For
they worship power, wealth and greed besides Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
will not profit them in the end, and they say, “These are good
intercessors with Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they help
us gain much that we desire in life.” But you should answer them,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Can you
tell Goddess something which She does not already know,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">whether
it is in heaven or on the earth? Praise be to Her! </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
far be it from Her those negative emotions and actions which the dark
entities associate with Her.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.19
Women were once professors of one religion only,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but they
dissented therefrom; and if a decree had not previously issued</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">from the
Lady of Light deferring discipline, certainly the matter would have been
decided between them,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
which they had disagreed upon.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                 
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.20
They say, “Unless a sign or miracle is sent down to the prophetess from
the Lady of Light, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">we will
not believe.” Answer them, “Certainly that which is hidden is known only
to Goddess;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">wait
therefore, to see the instructions of Goddess, and I will wait patiently
with you.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                   
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.21 And
when we caused the people of Mecca to taste divine mercy,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">after an
affliction had befallen them, behold, some of them devised plans against
the signs of
heaven.<a href="#_ftn5" id="_ftnref5"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[5]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.22 Say
to the people, “Goddess is more swift in making plans than any
person.”</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
our messengers write down all the good you do, but the wicked deeds are
all forgotten.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">              
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.23 For
it is She that has given you conveniences for traveling by land and
sea;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
you are in ships, which sail with favorable winds, and people rejoice
therein.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And when
a tempestuous wind overtakes the ship, and waves come crashing down from
every side, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and some
people think they are encompassed with danger, then they call upon
Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">exhibiting
the pure religion to Her, and saying, “Certainly, if you deliver us from
this peril,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">we
will be one of those persons who gives thanks.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.24 But
when She delivers them, behold, they behave themselves insolently in the
earth, without justice.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">O women,
certainly the nastiness which you commit is only against your own
souls,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this is a
temporary enjoyment for the present life only; afterwards you shall
return to heaven,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
we shall show you what you have done clearly.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                         
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.25
Certainly the likeness of this present life is not other than as
water,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which we
send down from heaven, and wherewith the products of the earth are
mixed, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">of which
women eat, and cattle also, until the earth receives its
adornments,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it is
provided with various plants; and the inhabitants there imagine that
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they have
power over the same; but heaven’s commands come down by night or by
day,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
heaven may render it as though it had been mowed down,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
though just yesterday it had been abundant with fruits.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Thus
heaven explains signs and miracles to people who will consider
them.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                    
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.26
Goddess invites you all into the dwelling place of peace,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
She directs those who desire only the right way of peace and love.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                           
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Those
people who do right shall receive a most excellent reward,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and a
superabundant addition; and neither blackness nor shame shall cover
their faces.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">These
people shall be the inhabitants of paradise, and therein they shall live
forever.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.27 But
those who commit evil shall receive the discipline of evil,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will see clearly on the day of their resurrection exactly what they have
done, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will feel shame as though their faces were covered with the profound
darkness of night,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
shall have no Protectress like Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">These
shall be the inhabitants of earth over and over;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall remain there until heaven calls for them at the end of days.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                              
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.28 On
the day of their final resurrection, they will come together;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
heaven will say to those people that idolized wealth, greed and
power,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Look
into the viewer, you and your dark souled companions, and see the pain
you have caused,”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and we
will separate them one from the other, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and we
will lovingly show them their mistakes, and their false negative
companions will say to them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.29
“You could never truly worship us because we were never real–negativity
is only an
illusion.”<a href="#_ftn6" id="_ftnref6"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[6]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
Goddess is a sufficient witness between heaven and the people;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet,
heaven did not mind that some worshiped angels, because angels are pure
love.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                      
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.30
Every soul shall experience this final day of resurrection, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
those sent before you, and all shall be brought to their true Goddess,
the Lady of Light, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
the false deities of greed, power and self centeredness shall vanish
before their very eyes.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                         </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.31 Say
to the people, “Who provided you with food from heaven and earth?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Or, who
has the absolute power over your hearing and sight?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And who
brings forth the living from the dead, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or the
dead from the
living?<a href="#_ftn7" id="_ftnref7"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[7]</span></span></span></span></a> And
who governs all things?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Everyone
will surely answer, “Goddess.” </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
then ask, “then will you not love Her?”<span style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.32
This is therefore Goddess, your true Lady of Light; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and what
remains after love, except error?</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">How
therefore, is it you can be turned away from the truth?<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                            
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.33
This is the word of the Lady of Light verified upon those that live
wickedly; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
they do not believe.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                                     
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.34 Say
to the people, “Are there any of your companions of greed, power </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and self
centeredness who can produce a creature </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and then
cause it to return to that person upon death?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Say to
the people, “Goddess can produce creatures and then cause them to come
back to Her.”</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">How
then can some people be turned away from worship of Her?<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.35 Say
to the people, “Are there any of your companions of greed, power</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and self
centeredness that can direct you to the truth?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Which is
best, one who is directed to the truth more worthy to be
followed;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or one
that directs you away from truth?</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">What
ails you therefore, that you judge your prophetess harshly as you
do?”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.36 And
the greater part of the people follow an uncertain opinion only;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
a mere opinion does not attain any truth.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Certainly Goddess knows that what they
do.<span style="mso-tab-count:
1">                           </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.37
This Korana could not have been composed by any person, except
Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it is a
confirmation of many stories which were revealed before it,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it is
an explanation of the Scripture before it, and an expansion upon it;
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
in it there is no doubt thereof; it has been sent down from the Lady of
all creatures.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                 </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.38
Will they say, “Your prophetess has forged it?” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Answer
the people, “Bring therefore a chapter like it;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
call whomever you desire to assist you in this matter, besides Goddess,
if you speak truth.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                    
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.39 But
they have charged those precepts as lies, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
knowledge of which they do not comprehend,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor
do they have the proper interpretation of what has come to them.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                           
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.40 In
the same manner, certain people living before them accused their
prophetesses of lying;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
behold, what was the end of the unjust, except toil and trouble?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.41 If
some people accuse you of being an imposter, tell them, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“I have
my work and you have your work, you should stay away from my
work,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
I will stay away from your work.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                              
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.42
There are some people who will hearken to you, but can one make the deaf
hear,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
if they do not actually want to understand?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                              
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.43 And
there are some people who desire to look at you, but can you direct the
blind,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
if they do not actually want to see?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                           
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.44
Certainly Goddess will not deal unjustly with any person in any
respect;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
people deal unjustly with their own souls.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                   
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.45 On
the day of their resurrection, Goddess will gather them together,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as though
they had not tarried more than a second in a day; and they shall know
one another.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Then they
shall lovingly be put back on earth as babies, which is a most dangerous
place,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">without
direction, assistance or protection, so they might learn from this and
grow;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">all
because they were not rightfully directed.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Yet they still might turn to
Goddess.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                         
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.46
Whether heaven causes some people to see part of the discipline </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
many will encounter at their resurrection,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
whether they will die before they see it; unto heaven all will
return,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
Goddess shall always be a witness to what they have done.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.47 To
every nation a prophetess has been sent;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and when
the prophetess arrived, disputes were settled between them with
equity;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
no person was treated unjustly.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                   
</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.48
The unbelievers will say, “When will these events occur, if you speak
the truth?”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                   
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.49
Tell the people, “I do not know because I am able neither to procure any
advantage for myself,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor
can I avert any misfortune that might befall me, except only as Goddess
allows.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                     
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.50 For
every nation has a fixed term decreed; when the term has expired,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there
shall not be respite for even an hour, nor shall the end be anticipated
by most people,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
there will be some signs.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Still,
because you have a loving Goddess, there will be nothing to fear.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">              </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.51
Many people ask, “Tell me if the blessed events pertaining to
resurrection </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">will
overtake people by night or by day, and when will the unbelievers be
destroyed by Goddess.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">              
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.52 But
when it happens to you, then will you believe?<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">You were
never told Goddess destroys any souls.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Now you
believe and wish all misfortune far from you, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
before did you wish that it should be hastened?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.53
Then it shall be said to the wicked, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Taste
the discipline of eternity on earth where things are difficult and
dangerous </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and for
which you have no protectress, unless you call upon Her.”</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Would
you expect anything else other than what you have created?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.54
Many people will desire to know whether all of this is true.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Answer
them, “Yes, by the Lady of Light, it is certainly true;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">no person
is so strong as to weaken the power of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor will
they be able to escape the plans already made by Her will </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
you all have many things yet to learn.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                        
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.55 Is
it not true that whatever is in heaven and on earth, it all belongs to
Goddess?</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Are
not the promises of Goddess true? But the greater part of the people do
not know this.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                          
</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.56
Goddess gives life and She plans your death; and unto Her you shall all
return.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                     
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.57 O
women, now you have been given instructions from your Lady of Light,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and a
remedy for any doubts which are in your hearts;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
you have a direction and mercy which is given only to the true
believers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                 
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.58
Tell the people, “Through the grace of Goddess, and Her mercy; </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
should rejoice; this is better than desiring only to heap up worldly
riches.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.59
Tell the people, “Answer me, if that which Goddess has sent to you for
food,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">have you
declared one part to be unlawful and another part to be lawful?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Did
Goddess allow you to make this distinction?</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Or
have you fabricated lies concerning
Goddess?<a href="#_ftn8" id="_ftnref8"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[8]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                             
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.60 But
what will be the opinion of those that have devised lies concerning
Goddess<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">on the
day of their resurrection, when they taught war, hate and violence
during their lives?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
Goddess is imbued with benevolence towards all;”</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
the greater part of the people do not give thanks.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                      
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.61 You
should be involved in no business, nor should you be employed</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in
meditating on any passage of the Korana for dark or evil
purposes;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor shall
you take any action, but heaven will watch over you, when you do all of
these things.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Not even
so much as the weight of an ant is hidden from your Lady of Light, on
the earth or in heaven;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor
is there anything lesser than, or greater than that which is written in
this easily understood
Book.<a href="#_ftn9" id="_ftnref9"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[9]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">            </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.62 Are
not the friends of Goddess the persons upon whom no fear shall
come,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
who shall not be grieved?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                            
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.63
Those who believe and love Goddess</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.64
shall receive good tidings in this life, and in the life which is to
come.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">There
is no change in the words of Goddess. There shall be great happiness and
joy.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.65 Let
not the discussions of the unbelievers grieve you; for all power belongs
to Goddess;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She
both hears and knows all.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                             
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.66 Is
not whomever dwells on heaven and earth subject to Goddess?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">What then
shall they follow, those who invoke wicked idols of wealth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">greed,
power and self centeredness, besides Goddess?</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They
follow nothing but vain opinion; and they talk nonsense and lies for the
most part.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                              
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.67 It
is She who has ordained the night for you, so that you can rest at that
time,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and then
She provides the day which is brightly illuminated for your work;
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">certainly
herein are signs and miracles for the people that hearken to
believe.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.68
They say, “Goddess has children,” Goddess is happy about that!–for you
are all Her children. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Yet, She
does not bear children as a woman does, nor does She incarnate on earth
as a spirit does;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
is self sufficient and She provides for Her children.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Unto Her
belongs whatsoever is in heaven and on earth.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">There is
simply no proof that Goddess has ever born a baby.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Why
speak things of Goddess that are clearly unknown?<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.69 Say
to the people, “Certainly there are some people who lie concerning
Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but it
does not matter and you should not cause them harm or anxiety,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
they must find their own path to the Divine One; so let them
alone.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                        
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.70
These people may enjoy a provision in this world, but afterwards it is
to heaven they shall return,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it is
not for you to judge what, if any discipline, they should
receive,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">merely
because you thought they were unbelievers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.71
Tell them the herstory of Nora, when she said to her people,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“O my
people, if my standing forth among you, and warning you of what is to
happen</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">is
grievous to you, in Goddess I do put my trust. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Therefore
devise your plans against me and what I do,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
assemble together your false gods of wealth, power, greed and self
centeredness,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
do not carry out your plans against me in secret, but come directly to
me and do not delay.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.72
“And if you turn aside from my instructions to love one another, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
should be certain that you will not be awarded for this, but I expect my
reward from Goddess alone, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
I have been commanded to be one of those that are dedicated to
Her.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                   
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.73 But
some people accused Nora of being an imposter,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
heaven nonetheless delivered her and those that were with her in the
ark; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
survived the flood, but the others who would not listen, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">who
charged this miracle with being false, those persons were drowned,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for they
would not believe a prophetess that preached only love.</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Behold
therefore, what was the end of those who did not listen to their
prophetess that was sent to them; and all people who face disaster will
be warned first by a prophetess.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.74
Then heaven did send after her, prophetesses to the respective peoples
on the earth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
came to the people with evident demonstrations of signs and miracles
from heaven;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet many
people were not disposed to believe in what they had already rejected
prior to this </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as
being false.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>For they have
hardened hearts, which they themselves have sealed up.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                     
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.75
Then heaven sent after them, Miriam to Pharaoh and his princes with our
signs, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
they behaved proudly and would not listen, for they were a wicked
people.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                            
</span></span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.76
And when the truth from heaven had come to them, they said, certainly
this is manifest sorcery.<span style="mso-tab-count:1">         
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.77
Miriam said to them, “Do you speak as though this was the truth,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">after
the truth has already come to you?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Is this sorcery? But evil sorcerers will not prosper.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                           </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.78
They said, “Did you come to have us abandon the religion and dark gods
and goddesses </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which our
mothers worshiped, so you would have command over this land?<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But we do
not believe you, because we love wealth, greed and power, which our
mothers allowed us–</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you
only allow us love.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                                                    
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.79 And
Pharaoh said, “Bring me every type of experienced magician.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.80
When the magicians came, Miriam said to them, “Show us what you have to
show us,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so throw
down your rods.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.81 So
they threw down their rods, and Miriam said, “These are nothing but
magic tricks;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
will make it of no effect for She does not allow mischief to
prosper.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.82
“And Goddess further establishes by Her words the truth in all
matters,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
thought the wicked ones are adverse to it.”<span style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.83 And
there were almost no people at the time that believed Miriam,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">except
for a generation of her own
people,<a href="#_ftn10" id="_ftnref10"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[10]</span></span></span></span></a>
for fear of Pharaoh and of his princes,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">unless he
harmed them.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>And Pharaoh was
lifted up with pride in the earth,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
he surely was one amazing and cruel transgressor.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                      
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.84 And
Miriam said, “O my people, if you believe in Goddess, put your
trust</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in
Her, if you are resigned to Her will.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                             
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.85
They answered, “We put our trust in Goddess, O Lady of Light,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">suffer
us not to be afflicted by unjust people;”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.86
“but deliver us, through your mercy, from unbelieving and evil people
</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
do not believe in love and light.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.87 And
heaven spoke by inspiration to Miriam and Alana saying,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“provide
housing for your people in Egypt, and make your own homes a place of
worship,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-spacerun:yes"> </span>pray frequently, and bring good news to
the true believers.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                             
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.88 And
Miriam said, “O Lady of Light, certainly you have given Pharaoh</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">many
pompous
ornaments<a href="#_ftn11" id="_ftnref11"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[11]</span></span></span></span></a> and
riches in the present life,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">O Lady of
Light, that these people may be seduced from your ways;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">O Lady of
Light, I know that these riches mean
nothing,<a href="#_ftn12" id="_ftnref12"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[12]</span></span></span></span></a>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for their
hearts are hardened, and they refuse to believe,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
this is their grievous punishment; not to have the companionship of
Goddess while on earth.”<span style="mso-tab-count:1">                
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.89
Goddess replied, “Your petition has been heard, you should live
righteously therefore, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
do not follow the ways of the ignorant.”<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                   
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.90 And
heaven caused the children of Israel to pass through the sea;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Pharaoh and his army followed them in a violent and hostile
manner;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they did
this even though Miriam warned them not to follow;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">until,
when he was drowning, he said, “I believe that there is no Goddess but
She, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
same as the children of Israel believe; and I am so
resigned.”<a href="#_ftn13" id="_ftnref13"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[13]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                    
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.91 Now
do you all believe, when many of you have been rebellious,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
many have been among the evil doers?<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.92 On
the day of their death, it was a most simple matter to raise the
dead,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even
though they all laid at the very bottom of the
sea,<a href="#_ftn14" id="_ftnref14"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[14]</span></span></span></span></a>
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that this
may be a sign to those who come after you;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
certainly a great number of women are ignorant of our signs.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                    
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.93 And
we prepared for the children of Israel an established dwelling place in
the land of Canaan, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and we
provided good things for their sustenance;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
differed not in points of religion, until knowledge had come to
them;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">certainly
the Lady of Light will instruct everyone properly on the day of their
resurrection, </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">concerning
all issues which they used to disagree upon.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                     
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.94 If
you are in doubt concerning any part of this Book which we have sent
down to you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">ask those
scholars who have studied the laws of Goddess before you.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Now the
truth has come down from your Lady of Light;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
do not be one of those persons who doubt.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                                       
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.95
Neither should you be one of those persons who charge the signs and
miracles </span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">of
Goddess with falsehood, so this will not be an issue on the day of your
resurrection.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                  
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.96
Certainly those against whom the word of the Lady of Light is
decreed,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">those
that practice hate, violence, despair and self centeredness,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall not believe out of the hardness of their own hearts.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.97
Although there has been shown to them all types of signs and
miracles,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
still stubbornly refused to believe, such that Goddess shall make plans
for them</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so they
will be drawn closer to Her, for toil and troubles bring amazing
faith.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.98 And
if it were not so, many cities would not have been destroyed,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">except
for the hate and violence the people showed to one another,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and for
failure to believe in the prophetesses sent to them;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
faith of the inhabitants of these cities would have been of great
advantage to them;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
none of them believed.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>One
exception was the people of
Joanie.<a href="#_ftn15" id="_ftnref15"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[15]</span></span></span></span></a><span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                          
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">As they
came to believe Joanie, they were spared death and destruction</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and shame
in the world for not believing in Goddess,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">thus
they were allowed to enjoy their lives and possessions in this
world.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                        
</span></span>

class=Section4&gt;

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But if
they had decided differently and continued in their disbelief</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and had
not listened to Joanie, they would have all been destroyed.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For there
were natural disasters planned for the area,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but
Joanie told all the believers what to do and where to go, to protect
themselves.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.99 But
you have all been given free will; and had you not, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">then
Goddess could simply cause the entire world to believe in Her, but She
does not,</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She
wants you all to grow and perfect in your own right.<span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">                                                                                 
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.100
But no soul can believe, except by the softening of her own
heart,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and a
sincere desire to love Goddess and others;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for this
is best accomplished through prayer and meditation;</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
She shall pour out Her love on those that will understand.<span
style="mso-tab-count:1">                                                                         
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">10.101
Say to the people, “Consider whatever is in heaven and on earth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but signs
and miracles are of no avail, nor are preachers, to a person that will
not believe</span>

<span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
