she continued her journey from south to north, until she came between
two sets of mountains,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.93 and
she found yet a third tribe, one that could barely understand her
language.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.94 And
they said, “O great ruler, Gog and
Magog<a href="#_ftn133" id="_ftnref133"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[133]</span></span></span></span></a>
have wasted our land,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">might we
pay a tribute to you so that you could build a great barrier between us
and them?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.95 She
answered, “The power which my Lady of Light has strengthened me with
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">is better
than your payment, but help me vigorously, and I will set a strong wall
between you and them.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.96
“Bring me iron in large pieces, until it fills up the spaces between the
two sides of the mountains.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And she
said to the workers, “Blow with your bellows, until it makes the iron
red hot.”<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And she
said further, “Bring me molten brass, that we may pour this over all of
the iron.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.97
Wherefore, when this wall was complete, Gog and Magog could not scale
it,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor could
they dig under it or through
it.<a href="#_ftn134" id="_ftnref134"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[134]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.98 The
ruler then said to them, “This is a mercy from my Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but when
the prediction of my Lady of Light shall come to be fulfilled,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the wall
will be reduced to dust, the people will war no longer, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
prediction of my Lady of Light is true.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.99 On
that day, the people will rise up and rejoice, like waves on an
ocean,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
trumpet shall sound, and all the people will gather in one body together
in love.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.100
And as to those who believed in hell and punishment,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.101
their eyes will be opened and they will see the love of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for their
eyes were veiled from remembering this, and they could not hear Her
words.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.102 Do
the unbelievers think that Goddess will not love them and care for
them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">because
they will take Evil for a protectress besides Me?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Although
many would like to believe it,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there is
no hell prepared as an abode for the infidels or the unfaithful,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for we
have more sophisticated plans for them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to
cleanse their souls, provide them with experience and draw them closer
to Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.103
Say to the people, “Does heaven need to declare outright to you</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">those
whose works are in vain,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.104
those whose endeavors in the present life have been wrongly
directed,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
who think they do the work of what is right, so you will know
plainly?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.105
There are many who do not believe in the signs and miracles of the Lady
of Light, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and when
they appear before Her, they will know that works of evil are in
vain,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and evil
works will not be accorded any weight on the day of their
resurrection.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.106
This is not a reward, it is an assistance to the development of the
soul.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And while
life on earth is like hell, there is no other hell,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for those
that have disbelieved and did not understand Her miracles</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and Her
prophetesses will come to understand all this later,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but they
will all pass through many trials and tribulations along the way.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.107
But as for those who believe and do good works,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
shall have the gardens of paradise for their eternal abode.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.108
They shall remain there forever, they will never desire any change
therefrom.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.109
Say to the people, “If the sea became as ink to write down all the words
of the Lady of Light, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it would
run out, and this would happen, even if heaven were to provide </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">an equal
amount of sea as ink for a writing supply to Goddess.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">18.110
Say to the people, “Certainly I am only a woman, as you are.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It has
been revealed to me that your Goddess is only one Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">let her
who hopes to meet her Lady of Light do righteous works,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and let
her not make any other person who does not desire it, worship the Lady
of Light.<span style="mso-tab-count:2">              </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:17.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚‚</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">BOOK
NINETEEN--ENTITLED MOTHER MARY</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">REVEALED
AT MECCA</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">In the
name of the most Merciful Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.1
K.H.Y.A.S.<a href="#_ftn135" id="_ftnref135"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[135]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
is Sufficient, the True Guide, the Bestower of Mercy to all.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.2 This
is a commemoration of the mercy of the Lady of Light toward Anna
and<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Zacharias.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.3 When
Anna called upon the Lady of Light, invoking Her in secret,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.4 she
said, “O Lady of Light, certainly my bones are weak, my head has become
white,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but I
have never been unsuccessful in my prayers to You, O Lady of
Light.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.5 “But
now I fear my nieces, who will succeed me, for my husband is
impotent,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">wherefore,
give me a successor of my own body out of Your Love.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.6
“That She might be my heir, and She may be an heir to the family of
Jacklyn,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and grant
me O Lady of Light, that she will be acceptable to You.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.7 And
an angel answered her, “O Anna, certainly we bring you good tidings of
the birth of a daughter,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">whose
name shall be Jane, and there has lived no one with this name
before.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.8 And
Anna said to the Lady of Light, “How shall I have a daughter, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">seeing
that my husband is impotent,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and I am
now very old, and I am also frail.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.9 The
angel said, “So it shall be: your Lady of Light has spoken and said,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">‘this is
easy for me, since I created you before, when you were just a divine
spark.’”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.10
Anna said, “O Lady of Light, please grant me a sign.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The angel
replied, “Your husband will not be able to speak for three nights,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">although
he is in perfect health.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.11 And
she went to her husband and her people, telling them this,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and her
husband had already quit being able to speak, for no apparent
reason.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But her
husband, being a believer, went forth making signs to the people,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as if he
should say, “Praise Goddess,” in the morning and in the evening.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.12 And
we said to her daughter, “O Jane, receive the Book of the law, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to study
it and to observe it.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And we
bestowed on her great wisdom, while she was still a child.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.13 And
she received mercy from us, and purity of life, and she was a devout
person,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.14 and
she was dutiful toward her parents, and she was not proud or
rebellious.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.15
Peace was upon her the day she was born, and the day whereupon she would
die,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
day that she would be raised to eternal life.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.16 And
remember in the Book of the Korana, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the story
of Mother Mary, when she left her family to a place in the east,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.17 she
took a veil to conceal her and her husband from the people, so they
might be in peace,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and we
sent our spirit Gabrielle to her, and she appeared to her in the shape
of a perfect woman, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so as not
to make her afraid.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.18 But
she was afraid of the strange Light Being and said,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“I desire
to fly for refuge to the Merciful Goddess, that She may defend me from
you;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if you
love Goddess, you will not approach nearer to me.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.19 She
answered, “Certainly I am a messenger of the Lady of Light </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and I am
sent here to give you a holy child.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.20 She
replied, “How could that be that I should have a son,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">since I
have not been with a man and I am chaste.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.21
Gabrielle replied, “It shall be.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>For everything is simple and easy for the Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
heaven shall do it, and this will be a sign to the people, and a mercy
from us,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for it is
an event miracle which has been decreed.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.22
Therefore she conceived a son, and she went away with him in her womb to
a distant place,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.23 and
the pains of childbirth came upon her near the trunk of a palm
tree.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She said,
in her great pain, “I wish to Goddess that I had died before this,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and had
become a thing forgotten, and lost in oblivion,”.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.24 And
she heard from beneath her, a voice saying, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Do not
be grieved, for Goddess has given you a river under you.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.25 and
you should shake the body of the palm tree, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it
will let fall ripe dates for you, easy to gather.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.26 You
should eat and drink and calm your mind. Also, if you see any person,
and they ask you, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">reply
that you have vowed silence to honor the Merciful Lady, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and that
you will speak to no one today.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.27 So
she brought the child to her people, carrying him in her arms.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They said
to her, “O Mary, how have you done this strange thing?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.28
“Understand that your father was a faithful and chaste husband, and so
was your mother.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.29 But
she made signs to the child to answer them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but they
said, “How could we speak to a child who is but an infant in the
cradle?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.30
Whereupon, the child said, “Certainly I am a servant of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She has
given me the Book of the gospel, and She has appointed me as Her
Prophet.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.31
“And She has made me blessed, wherever I am, and She has commanded me to
observe prayer,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and to
give alms, so long as I should live,”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.32
“and I will be dutiful towards my mother, and I will not be proud or
unhappy.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.33
“And peace shall be upon me the day when I was born, and on the day that
I will die,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and on
the day when I am raised to new life.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.34
This was Yeshua, the son of Mother Mary, the Word of Truth,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet many
will have great doubts concerning him.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.35 It
is not for you to debate whether Goddess has a son, Goddess forbid you
should hurt another!</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">When
Goddess decrees a thing, She need only say, “Be!” and it is.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.36 And
certainly Goddess is my Lady of Light and your Lady; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore,
serve Her, this is the right way.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.37 Yet
the religious sects differ among themselves concerning Yeshua,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but woe
shall come to those that are unbelievers, because of their appearance at
the last day.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.38 Do
you cause them to hear, or do you cause them to see?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">You will
not on the day where they will come to review their own lives;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but the
ungoddessly will see their obvious error on this day.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.39 But
you should warn them of the day of sighing, when the matter will be
shown to them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">although
now they are sunk in negligence, and do not believe.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.40
Certainly we will inherit the earth, and whatever creatures are therein,
and to us shall all return.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.41 And
remember Sarah in the Book of the Korana, for she was one of great
veracity, and a prophetess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.42
When she said to her father, “O my dear father,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">why do
you worship greed, wealth and power, how does it help you see or hear
better?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">How does
it profit your soul in the end?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.43 “O
my dear father, a degree of knowledge has been given to me,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which has
not been given to you, therefore follow me, and I will lead you to the
right way.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.44 “O
my father, serve not Evil, for Evil is not loved by Goddess.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.45 “O
my father, certainly I fear that you will suffer great trials</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
tribulations from the Merciful Lady because you find Evil to be a good
companion.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.46 Her
father answered, “Why do you reject my love of wealth and power,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">why do
you reject them, Sarah?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If you do
not refrain from continually chastising me, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">I will
surely stone you to death, therefore leave me alone for a long, long
while regarding this.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.47
Sarah replied, “Peace be upon you, I will ask pardon for you from my
Lady of Light, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for She
is most gracious to me.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.48
“And I will separate myself from you, at your request, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and I
will not love wealth and power as you do, and I will call upon my Lady
of Light;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">however,
it may be that I will not be as unsuccessful in calling upon my
Lady,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">as you
are successful at putting your trust in what you desire.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.49 And
when she separated herself from her father, and from his worship of
wealth and power, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">she was
given Iris and Jacklyn, each of them we made prophetesses.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.50 And
we bestowed upon them, through our mercy, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the gift
of prophecy, and children and wealth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and we
caused them to deserve the highest commendations, and they did this all
very well.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.51 And
remember Miriam in the Book of the Korana,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for she
was sincerely
upright,<a href="#_ftn136" id="_ftnref136"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:
footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[136]</span></span></span></span></a>
and was an apostle and a prophetess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.52 And
we called to her from the right side of Mt. Sinai,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
caused her to draw near, and to speak with us privately. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.53 And
we gave her through our mercy, a sister Alana, a prophetess, for her
assistant.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.54
Remember also Emma in the same Books, for she was true to her promise
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and was
an apostle and a prophetess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.55 And
she showed her family that to observe prayer and to give alms is good,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and she
was acceptable to her Lady of Light.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.56 And
remember
Edna,<a href="#_ftn137" id="_ftnref137"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[137]</span></span></span></span></a> in
the same Book, for she was a just person, and a prophetess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.57 And
we exalted her to a high
place.<a href="#_ftn138" id="_ftnref138"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[138]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.58
There are those to whom Goddess has been bounteous, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">some of
the prophetesses of the posterity of Eve,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and there
are some born of the prophetesses of those carried in the ark with Nora,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and of
the posterity of Sarah, and of Isabell, and those that heaven directs
and has chosen.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">When the
signs of the Lady of Light were read to them, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they fell
down and began to worship Her, and they wept for joy,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.59 But
succeeding generations came after them, and their people neglected
prayer, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
followed lust and false idols, and they fell into evil.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.60
Except she who repents, believes and does what is right, those persons
shall enter paradise,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
shall not in the least be wronged.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.61
Gardens of perpetual abode will be their reward, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which the
Lady of Light has promised to Her servants, as an object of
faith,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for Her
promise will surely come to be fulfilled.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.62 At
that time there will be no more vain arguments,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">only
peace, and their provision will be prepared for them both morning and
evening.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.63<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>This is paradise, which heaven
provides for an inheritance, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for such
of Her servants which are pious.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.64 We
do not descend from heaven, unless by command of your Lady of
Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to Her
belongs whatsoever is before us, and whatsoever is behind us,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
whatsoever is in the intermediate space, nor is your Lady of Light ever
forgetful of you.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.65 She
is the Lady of heaven and of earth, and whatever is between them;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
worship Her and be frequent in prayer.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.66 Do
you know any creature named as well as She with so many wonderful
names?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.67
Some people say, “After I have died, shall I really be brought back
alive from the grave?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.68 Do
not the people remember that Goddess created them before, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">out of
nothing and surely She may easily do this again?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.69 But
the Lady of Light will assemble all the people together at the end of
time, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
will cleanse and purify the evil ones,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.70
After which, we will draw from every sect or kind, one representative
which was the best of them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">a kind
and caring person, one that was firmest in her love for Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.71 And
heaven knows best which are more worthy of glory; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and all
the true believers will be with
her<a href="#_ftn139" id="_ftnref139"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[139]</span></span></span></span></a>;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this is
an established decree with your Lady of Light.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.72
Afterwards, all will be delivered that have been pious,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but the
ungoddessly will be gathered together and left on their knees for
Goddess to come by them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
purify them with Her bright white light of holiness.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>And they will not suffer at
all.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.73
When our obvious signs are read to them, the unbelievers say, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Which of
the two types has more wealth and a better appearance?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.74 But
how many generations will it take before every person understands that
excelling in wealth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or
excelling in outward appearance is completely in vain?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.75 Say
to the people, “Even those that live in error, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">may very
well be granted a long life by the Lady of Light </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
they can see how the Lady of Light is a wonderful protectress, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that She
will bring them new life after death, that Her love is unending.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This is
so they will see who is in a stronger position, and who is in a weaker
one.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.76
Goddess only directs those that ask for Her direction,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
good works which they do will remain forever in the sight of the Lady of
Light, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">whereas
worldly possessions will not,<span style="mso-tab-count:1">           
</span> and with respect to a final reward, this is a far better
compensation.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.77
Have you seen a person that does not believe in </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the signs
and miracles of heaven, yet says that she will have riches and many
children, regardless?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.78 Is
she well acquainted with the secrets of the future,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or has
she received a covenant with the Lady of Light that it will be this
way?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.79 By
no means. Such words will not be recorded, but will be forgotten,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
person will continue to suffer trials and tribulations on earth without
a protectress.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.80 The
angels are heirs to everything on earth, and they write down all the
good works </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that are
done on this earth, and those that fail to do good works, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">will have
nothing good to review on the day of their resurrection, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will appear humble and in simple
garments.<a href="#_ftn140" id="_ftnref140"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[140]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.81
Such people take other negative goddesses of wealth, power and greed,
besides Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
glorify these empty things only, which will do them no good in the
end.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.82 By
no means is this the right way.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Once they have risen again,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they will
understand that such a lifetime was not any good, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will return to earth and hopefully exhort others to live in the right
way after this.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.83
Evil is always present around the infidels, because they call upon it
frequently, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they
incite themselves to sin by what they worship.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.84
Therefore do not be hasty to call Evil and destruction upon
yourselves,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for every
person has only a finite number of days of respite.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.85 On
a certain day, all the pious will be assembled together before Mother
Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">in an
honorable manner, as ambassadors called into the presence of their
Queen;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.86 and
the wicked will be purified, as thirsty cattle are driven to drink
water,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.87 the
time of intercession will be over and will no longer be needed,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
that have received further covenants from the Merciful Lady, will
receive them at that time.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.88
Some say that the Merciful Lady has begotten a child,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.89 but
She does not bear children as a woman does, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor is
She ever born to earth as souls are,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">although
She does send her Holy Spirit and Holy Ghost if you pray for them, these
are sent to the faithful. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And yet
some of you dispute over this, but it is not right to dispute to
hatred,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it is far
more important to love one another than to prove who is right. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.90 For
the heavens will never be truly be torn asunder, nor will the earth
truly cleave in half,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor will
the mountains ever be overthrown and fall such that you will be afraid
and worried,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but you
will find that what you see now really was an illusion and
unreal;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for the
Lady of Light does not intend to destroy any of you, nor frighten
you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for you
are all Her beloved children.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.91 The
destruction of the earth will never occur because</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">someone
says that Goddess has created a child that walked the earth.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.92 Why
is it all that you need to fight over whether or not She had a
child,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when your
lives are in such a disarray over hate, violence, rage, jealousy,
confusion</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
misunderstandings?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.93
Certainly, there is no entity in heaven or upon the earth,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that does
not approach Goddess as a servant and assistant.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.94
Goddess encompasses all things by Her infinite knowledge and
power,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
numbers everything with exact computation,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.95 and
every one shall come to Her on the day of her resurrection,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">without
any of their helpers and followers they worshiped as negative
idols.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.96 But
as for those who believe and do good works, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
Merciful Lady will bestow upon them love.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.97 We
have made the Korana easy for the tongue,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that you
may readily declare the promises of heaven to the pious,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
may denounce the beliefs among the people </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that
Goddess is mean, jealous, demanding and nasty; for She is not; She is
pure love.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">19.98 And
how many generations have we loved greatly </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that did
not return the love to Goddess and heaven?<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Yet She
perseveres in perfect love.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Although
you see them no more, She did not destroy even a single soul, for She
does not destroy souls.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">You may
not see the good ones any longer, but if you listen closely and become
alert to love,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">you may
be able to sense them around you still as your guardian angels.<span
style="mso-tab-count:3">                             </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
8">                                                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:15.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">ÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆ</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

</div>

<div style="mso-element:footnote-list">

style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">See
Table B, Introduction, page x.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn2" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref2" id="_ftn2"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[2]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Note
that in the Old Testament, Goddess had to rest after Her
creation.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn3" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref3" id="_ftn3"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[3]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
is referring to some Arabs that believed that demigods and demigoddesses
and angels and the like could intercede on the day of their resurrection
for them.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn4" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref4" id="_ftn4"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[4]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">These
are points in orbits or relative positions to the horizon.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn5" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref5" id="_ftn5"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[5]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For
it is said that the Meccans went through a time of famine, and they were
near perishing, so they turned to religion.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>However, when abundance was given back
to them, they went back to their old ways and continued to ridicule the
prophetess and her revelations.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn6" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref6" id="_ftn6"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[6]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said by some that on the last day that the negative idol worshipers
will all be gathered together before Goddess and that Goddess will cause
the idols to speak to them and the idols will then reproach the
worshipers instead of interceding for them because they only represented
the worst of human beings: greed, nastiness, unhappiness, etc..<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Others have claimed that the angels,
who were also worshiped by many are meant here, or will also be
included.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn7" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref7" id="_ftn7"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[7]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">To
bring forth the living from the dead is the resurrection to paradise,
and to bring forth the dead from the living is one’s death on
earth.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn8" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref8" id="_ftn8"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[8]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
people would draw lines in their orchards and where the fruit fell, they
would then declare accordingly what would belong to Goddess or the poor,
while the other belonged to the owner.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Not only did the prophetess notice that many people kept all the
good fruit anyway, but she found it to be a silly superstition that
would not always reflect a fair amount for both the owner and the
charitable recipient.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn9" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref9" id="_ftn9"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[9]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Referring
to the<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>“preserved table” where
all divine decrees are recorded.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn10" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref10" id="_ftn10"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[10]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
may refer to just some of the younger Israelites, or it may refer to
some of the younger Egyptians, including Asa, the wife of Pharaoh, who
believed in Miriam and her teachings of love and kindness.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Most likely it referred to some of the
Egyptians because Miriam was a great high priestess among the
Israelites.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn11" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref11" id="_ftn11"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[11]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Such
as fine chariots, homes, libraries, fancy clothes, etc.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn12" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref12" id="_ftn12"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[12]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
say at this comment all the treasures of the Egyptians were turned into
stone.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn13" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref13" id="_ftn13"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[13]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
say at this point, Gabrielle stopped up Pharaoh’s mouth with mud so he
could obtain no further mercy from Goddess, but of course archangels do
not do such things, for they are all peace and love.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn14" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref14" id="_ftn14"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[14]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
of the Israelite doubted that Pharaoh really drowned, so heaven caused
his body to float back to shore, with a coat of mail spun from fine gold
still on it to prove he had really drowned.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Others say he was naked.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn15" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref15" id="_ftn15"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[15]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">As
related in the story, the people of Ninevah (at the same or a location
close to al Mawsel is today), were extremely wicked and unfaithful.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>They were hostile and violent to one
another.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Joanie was sent by
Goddess to preach love and faith to them, but she had to leave the city
because they were so hostile to her.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>When she left, she warned them that their city would be destroyed
in 3 days, or as others relate, 40 days, and this would occur due to a
volcano or earthquake.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>But when
the time came near, the Ninevites saw the sky shoot forth fire and fill
the air with smoke, which hung directly over their city.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>They then went to the fields with
their families and cattle, and put on sack cloth and humbled themselves,
calling aloud for pardon, and sincerely repented to Goddess.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Whereupon, the land became
calm.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn16" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref16" id="_ftn16"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[16]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
possible interpretations for these initials are given in Table B,
introduction, page x</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn17" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref17" id="_ftn17"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[17]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For
the Ancient Arabs believe there is a throne which is held up by a spirit
or wind, with waters surrounding it, and this was created before the
heavens and earth.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The Jews have
also said that the throne of glory then stood in the air, and was borne
on the face of the waters, by the breath of Goddess.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn18" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref18" id="_ftn18"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[18]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">For
building an ark so far from water; and for becoming a carpenter and a
general contractor to the trades when she was formerly a prophetess and
high priestess.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn19" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref19" id="_ftn19"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[19]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
Arab legends tell of how a huge oven produced a flood of<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>boiling water over all<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>the land, and some say the waters that
rose were boiling hot.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Some say
the water was from Cufa in a spot where a Mosque now stands; other say
it came form India or Mesopotamia, and others say it was from an oven
that Eve used to bake her bread in and the oven was passed down from
generation to generation until it came to Nora, specifically for that
purpose.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It is also told that the
Persian Magi said the waters came from the oven of a certain old woman
named Zala Cufa.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>But the world
tannur, which was translated as oven, may also signify a spring or pool
of water.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn20" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref20" id="_ftn20"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[20]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Meaning
the daughters of Nora, their husbands and children</span><span
style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn21" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref21" id="_ftn21"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[21]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that it took 2 years to build the ark, which was framed of
Indian plane tree, it was divided into three stories, the lower was for
the animals, the middle one for people and the upper for the birds and
the body of Eve was taken on board.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>This seems to be a tradition of Eastern Christians, who believe
that spousal relations were suspended during the trip, though it is said
by some that a child was born upon the ark during the two years it
sailed.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn22" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref22" id="_ftn22"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[22]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is believed that only 8 people survived in the ark, just a few daughters
and their husbands and some children.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn23" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref23" id="_ftn23"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[23]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that the Chaldeans have the oldest stories regarding the
remainder of the ark, that it was last seen in the Gordyaean
mountains.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The inhabitants there
scraped the pitch off the planks and carried it about as an amulet.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Some say they used the wood of the
vessel against many diseases with great success.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The relics of the arks were also said
to be found in Epiphanius, and the emperor Heraclius took a journey and
saw the place of the ark.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The
Nestorians used to celebrate a feast day on the spot were the ark came
to rest, but in 776 CE, the monastery was destroyed by lightening
together with the church and many of the congregation in it.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>After this, it was said the ark rested
on Mt. Masis in Armenia.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Further,
the Ancient Arabs say the ark sailed on the tenth of Fajeb and came out
of it 6 months later on the tenth of al Moharram, which became a feast
day.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn24" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref24" id="_ftn24"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[24]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Meaning
“lily.”</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn25" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref25" id="_ftn25"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[25]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">By
giving you additional children.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn26" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref26" id="_ftn26"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[26]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Believed
to be the best way to hold an animal, rendering it helpless.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn27" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref27" id="_ftn27"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[27]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">One
commentator had said that Sarah laugh at the angels discovering
themselves and the removing all fears from their thoughts; others say
she laughed at the approaching destruction of the wicked townspeople;
others say her menstruation, which had stopped for many years, came upon
her suddenly and that caused her to laugh, which is quite
strange.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn28" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref28" id="_ftn28"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[28]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">At
this time it was reported that Sarah was 90 or 99 years old, and her
husband was 120 years old.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn29" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref29" id="_ftn29"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[29]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">When
Asians meet, after having made the ordinary salutation, “Peace be with
you,” they move the hand to the left side and mutually shake hands.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>When they are very intimate they
repeat this ceremony, and wish good wishes to one another.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If they do not know someone very well,
they merely give her the salutation, and if it is an unbeliever, they
content themselves by saying “good day.”<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Sarah, seeing that the two angels did not touch her hand,
concluded they were strangers.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn30" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref30" id="_ftn30"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[30]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Note
that Sarah and Wileh are contemporaries in the Korana.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn31" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref31" id="_ftn31"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[31]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Because
only unbelievers do such things.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn32" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref32" id="_ftn32"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[32]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
say that Nora’s husband was killed when he turned back due to his
infidelity in not listening to his prophetess wife.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Others say that Gabrielle lifted her
wing and picked up the offending cities and dropped them back to earth,
destroying everything and everyone.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>They were said to have been lifted so high that the inhabitants
of the lower heaven heard the barking of the dogs and the crowing of the
roosters.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Of course this is a
mere tale or allegory because angels are all peace and love and do not
do such things.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn33" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref33" id="_ftn33"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[33]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Said
by some to have been baked in hell.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Of course, hell is simply an allegory. Earth is hell.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn34" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref34" id="_ftn34"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[34]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Said
by some to have marking of white and red or some other marking to
distinguish them from other stones; others still say that the stones
were marked with the names of the people they were meant to kill.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>But Goddess does not kill or maim
anyone so this is clear allegory.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn35" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref35" id="_ftn35"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[35]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
original word was “daif” which meant blind, and some believed that this
prophetess was blind and therefore disqualified from being holy and/or a
priestess.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn36" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref36" id="_ftn36"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
